My biggest problem is Rickje himself. For the thousands upon thousands of robux that has been donated to the man, nothing has even been added. I am disappointed that the game has gotten this low with copiers, toxicity, and most importantly, arrogance. I will continue to make content, but with War Thunder quickly overtaking my playing schedule, I will not upload as often. School is also a huge thing that has not allowed me to create content. Back to plane crazy, BUILDING IS REPETITIVE. All it is is to use motor lock techniques to create a very low performing, high quality jet. I am honestly sick of the game I put so much work and time into and it results with no rewarding aspects.
